```json
{
  "command": "$REPO = \"edburns/Build26-BRK206-your-agent-anywhere-multiclient-multidevice-with-github-copilot-sdk\"\n$PR = 22\n$TIMEOUT = 600\n$INTERVAL = 30\n$ELAPSED = 0\n\nwhile ($ELAPSED -lt $TIMEOUT) {\n    # Strategy A: \"Copilot's findings\"\n    $FINDINGS = gh api \"/repos/$REPO/pulls/$PR/reviews\" --jq '.[] | select(.body | test(\"Copilot.s findings\")) | {id: .id, body: .body}' 2>$null | Select-Object -Last 1\n\n    # Strategy B: \"Pull request overview\"\n    if (-not $FINDINGS) {\n        $FINDINGS = gh api \"/repos/$REPO/pulls/$PR/reviews\" --jq '.[] | select(.body | test(\"Pull request overview\")) | {id: .id, body: .body}' 2>$null | Select-Object -Last 1\n    }\n\n    # Strategy C: copilot-pull-request-reviewer bot\n    if (-not $FINDINGS) {\n        $FINDINGS = gh api \"/repos/$REPO/pulls/$PR/reviews\" --jq '.[] | select(.user.login | test(\"copilot-pull-request-reviewer\")) | {id: .id, body: .body}' 2>$null | Select-Object -Last 1\n    }\n\n    # Strategy D: Line-level comments from Copilot\n    if (-not $FINDINGS) {\n        $FINDINGS = gh api \"/repos/$REPO/pulls/$PR/comments\" --jq '.[] | select(.user.login == \"Copilot\") | {id: .id, body: .body}' 2>$null | Select-Object -First 1\n    }\n\n    if ($FINDINGS) {\n        Write-Host \"Copilot review found after ${ELAPSED}s\"\n        Write-Host $FINDINGS\n        break\n    }\n\n    Write-Host \"[$ELAPSED s] Waiting for Copilot review...\"\n    Start-Sleep -Seconds $INTERVAL\n    $ELAPSED += $INTERVAL\n}\n\nif (-not $FINDINGS) {\n    Write-Host \"TIMEOUT: No Copilot review after ${TIMEOUT}s\"\n}",
  "description": "Poll for Copilot code review agent to post",
  "mode": "sync",
  "initial_wait": 120
}

{
  "command": "$REPO = \"edburns/Build26-BRK206-your-agent-anywhere-multiclient-multidevice-with-github-copilot-sdk\"\n$BRANCH = \"copilot/work\"\n$PR = 22\n$TIMEOUT = 600\n$INTERVAL = 30\n$ELAPSED = 0\n\nwhile ($ELAPSED -lt $TIMEOUT) {\n    # Check for new workflow runs on copilot/work branch\n    $runs = gh run list -R $REPO --branch $BRANCH --json databaseId,status,conclusion,name --jq '.[] | {name,status,conclusion}'\n    Write-Host \"[$ELAPSED s] Runs: $runs\"\n\n    # Strategy A/B/C checks for reviews\n    $FINDINGS = gh api \"/repos/$REPO/pulls/$PR/reviews\" --jq '.[] | select(.body | test(\"Copilot.s findings|Pull request overview\")) | {id: .id}' 2>$null\n    if (-not $FINDINGS) {\n        $FINDINGS = gh api \"/repos/$REPO/pulls/$PR/reviews\" --jq '.[] | select(.user.login | test(\"copilot-pull-request-reviewer\")) | {id: .id}' 2>$null\n    }\n    if (-not $FINDINGS) {\n        $FINDINGS = gh api \"/repos/$REPO/pulls/$PR/comments\" --jq '.[] | select(.user.login == \"Copilot\") | {id: .id}' 2>$null\n    }\n\n    if ($FINDINGS) {\n        Write-Host \"Review found!\"\n        break\n    }\n\n    Start-Sleep -Seconds $INTERVAL\n    $ELAPSED += $INTERVAL\n}\nif (-not $FINDINGS) { Write-Host \"TIMEOUT: No review after ${TIMEOUT}s\" }",

{"body":"Trimming the bounded `events` list with `while (events.size() \u003e MAX_EVENTS) { events.remove(0); }` can be unnecessarily expensive on `CopyOnWriteArrayList` because each `remove(0)` forces an array copy/shift. ```json
{
  "command": "$REPO = \"edburns/Build26-BRK206-your-agent-anywhere-multiclient-multidevice-with-github-copilot-sdk\"\n$BRANCH = \"copilot/work\"\n$PR = 22\n$TIMEOUT = 600\n$INTERVAL = 30\n$ELAPSED = 0\n\n# Track the existing review ID so we can detect a NEW one\n$EXISTING_REVIEW_ID = 4659126341  # from first round\n\nwhile ($ELAPSED -lt $TIMEOUT) {\n    # Check for new workflow run (code review in progress)\n    $runs = gh run list -R $REPO --branch $BRANCH --json databaseId,status,conclusion,name,createdAt --jq '.[] | select(.name == \"Running Copilot Code Review\") | {status,conclusion,created:.createdAt}'\n    Write-Host \"[$ELAPSED s] Code Review runs: $($runs -join ' | ')\"\n\n    # Check for new review (different from first round)\n    $NEW_REVIEW = gh api \"/repos/$REPO/pulls/$PR/reviews\" --jq \".[] | select(.id != $EXISTING_REVIEW_ID) | {id: .id, user: .user.login, state: .state}\" 2>$null\n    if ($NEW_REVIEW) {\n        Write-Host \"New review found: $NEW_REVIEW\"\n        break\n    }\n\n    Start-Sleep -Seconds $INTERVAL\n    $ELAPSED += $INTERVAL\n}\nif (-not $NEW_REVIEW) { Write-Host \"TIMEOUT or no new review after ${TIMEOUT}s\" }",
  "description": "Poll for second round Copilot code review",
  "initial_wait": 90,
  "mode": "sync"
}

Use `\u003ch:outputText\u003e` to ensure escaping is consistently applied.","id":3548321219,"in_reply_to_id":null,"line":null,"path":"src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/index.xhtml"}
{"body":"Trimming the bounded `events` list with `while (events.size() \u003e MAX_EVENTS) { events.remove(0); }` can be unnecessarily expensive on `CopyOnWriteArrayList` because each `remove(0)` forces an array copy/shift. Clearing the excess range in one operation avoids repeated copying and scales better if event volume increases.","id":3548321239,"in_reply_to_id":null,"line":262,"path":"src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/Agent.java"}
{"body":"`AppState` is `@ApplicationScoped`, so storing `selectedAgentId` here makes the “selected agent” a single global value shared across all browser sessions. In a multi-client demo this means one user’s click will change which agent details are rendered for every other connected user (and will be pushed to them via the shared refresh flow). Move selection state to a per-user scope (e.g., `@SessionScoped`/`@ViewScoped` backing bean) and have it look up the `Agent` in `AppState` rather than keeping the selection in application state.","id":3548361722,"in_reply_to_id":null,"line":35,"path":"src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/AppState.java"}
{"body":"This change triggers `notifyUi()` (which pushes a `:phase-changed` message) for every Copilot session event, not just actual phase changes. Because the client refresh cycle animates *all* cards on every `refreshPipeline()` completion, frequent non-phase events (tool calls/results, assistant messages, etc.) can cause constant re-render + animation churn and unnecessary server push traffic. Consider emitting a distinct push event type for “detail updated” (or throttling/batching updates) and only running the phase-change animation path when a real phase transition occurs.","id":3548361743,"in_reply_to_id":null,"line":132,"path":"src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/Agent.java"}

```
1. package com.microsoft.build.realestate;
2. 
3. import com.github.copilot.CopilotClient;
4. import com.github.copilot.CopilotClientMode;
5. import com.github.copilot.CopilotClientOptions;
6. import jakarta.annotation.PreDestroy;
7. import jakarta.enterprise.context.ApplicationScoped;
8. import jakarta.inject.Inject;
9. import java.nio.file.Path;
10. import java.util.Collection;
11. import java.util.Collections;
12. import java.util.Map;
13. import java.util.UUID;
14. import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
15. import java.util.logging.Logger;
16. 
17. /**
18.  * Application-scoped CDI bean that owns the CopilotClient and manages the
19.  * collection of active agent sessions.
20.  *
21.  * <p>Equivalent to the C# {@code AppState} class. All state is concurrent-safe
22.  * because multiple virtual threads may submit new enquiries simultaneously.
23.  */
24. @ApplicationScoped
25. public class AppState {
26. 
27.     private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(AppState.class.getName());
28. 
29.     /** How long (ms) a rejected agent stays visible before being removed. */
30.     private static final long REJECTED_LINGER_MS = 15_000L;
31. 
32.     private final CopilotClient copilotClient;
33.     private final Map<String, Agent> agents = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
34.     private volatile String selectedAgentId;
35. 
36.     @Inject
37.     private PropertyDatabase propertyDatabase;
38. 
39.     @Inject
40.     private UiUpdateSocket uiUpdateSocket;
41. 
42.     public AppState() {
43.         String copilotHome = Path.of(System.getProperty("user.home"), ".copilot").toString();
44.         this.copilotClient = new CopilotClient(
45.                 new CopilotClientOptions()
46.                         .setMode(CopilotClientMode.EMPTY)
47.                         .setCopilotHome(copilotHome));
48.     }
49. 
50.     /**
51.      * Submits a new enquiry and launches an agent session on a virtual thread.
52.      *
53.      * @param enquiry the customer's natural-language enquiry text
54.      * @return the new agent's ID
55.      */
56.     public String submitEnquiry(String enquiry) {
57.         String agentId = UUID.randomUUID().toString().replace("-", "").substring(0, 8);
58.         Agent agent = new Agent(agentId, enquiry, propertyDatabase, uiUpdateSocket);
59.         agents.put(agentId, agent);
60.         uiUpdateSocket.pushPhaseChange(agentId);
61. 
62.         Thread.ofVirtual().name("agent-" + agentId).start(() -> {
63.             try {
64.                 agent.run(copilotClient);
65.             } finally {
66.                 if (agent.isRejected()) {
67.                     scheduleRemoval(agentId);
68.                 }
69.             }
70.         });
71. 
72.         return agentId;
73.     }
74. 
75.     /** Returns an unmodifiable view of all current agents (active, done, and pending removal). */
76.     public Collection<Agent> getAgents() {
77.         return Collections.unmodifiableCollection(agents.values());
78.     }
79. 
80.     /** Returns the agent with the given ID, or {@code null} if not found. */
81.     public Agent getAgent(String agentId) {
82.         return agents.get(agentId);
83.     }
84. 
85.     public String getSelectedAgentId() {
86.         return selectedAgentId;
87.     }
88. 
89.     public void setSelectedAgentId(String selectedAgentId) {
90.         this.selectedAgentId = selectedAgentId;
91.     }
92. 
93.     public Agent getSelectedAgent() {
94.         if (selectedAgentId == null || selectedAgentId.isBlank()) {
95.             return null;
96.         }
97.         return agents.get(selectedAgentId);
98.     }
99. 
100.     /**
101.      * Schedules removal of a rejected agent after the linger period.
102.      * After removal, pushes an agent-removed event so the browser clears the card.
103.      */
104.     private void scheduleRemoval(String agentId) {
105.         Thread.ofVirtual().name("removal-" + agentId).start(() -> {
106.             try {
107.                 Thread.sleep(REJECTED_LINGER_MS);
108.             } catch (InterruptedException e) {
109.                 Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
110.                 return;
111.             }
112.             agents.remove(agentId);
113.             if (agentId.equals(selectedAgentId)) {
114.                 selectedAgentId = null;
115.             }
116.             uiUpdateSocket.pushAgentRemoved(agentId);
117.         });
118.     }
119. 
120.     @PreDestroy
121.     public void shutdown() {
122.         try {
123.             copilotClient.close();
124.         } catch (Exception e) {
125.             LOG.warning("Error closing CopilotClient: " + e.getMessage());
126.         }
127.     }
128. }
129.
```

19. public class PipelineView {

21.     private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(PipelineView.class.getName());
22.

24.     private AppState appState;
25.

34.     }

41.     }
42. 
43.     /**
44.      * Returns agents currently in a specific phase.
45.      */
46.     public List<Agent> getAgentsAtPhase(Phase phase) {
47.         return appState.getAgents().stream()
48.                 .filter(a -> a.getPhase() == phase)
49.                 .sorted(Comparator.comparing(Agent::getStartedAt))
50.                 .toList();
51.     }

55.     }

59.     }

63.     }
64.

66.      * JSF action method: submits the enquiry text to AppState and launches an agent.
67.      */
68.     public void submitEnquiry() {
69.         if (enquiryText == null || enquiryText.isBlank()) {
70.             FacesContext.getCurrentInstance().addMessage(null,
71.                     new FacesMessage(FacesMessage.SEVERITY_WARN,
72.                             "Please enter an enquiry.", null));
73.             return;
74.         }
75.         String agentId = appState.submitEnquiry(enquiryText.trim());
76.         LOG.info("Submitted enquiry, agent ID: " + agentId);
77.         enquiryText = "";
78.     }
79. 
80.     /**
81.      * Returns the CSS class(es) for a phase column header.
82.      * Used in index.xhtml to avoid complex inline EL ternary expressions.
83.      */
84.     public String getPhaseHeaderClass(Phase phase) {
85.         if (phase == Phase.DONE) {
86.             return "phase-header done";
87.         }
88.         if (phase.isRejected()) {
89.             return "phase-header rejected";
90.         }
91.         return "phase-header";
92.     }

94.     /**
95.      * Returns the CSS class(es) for an agent card based on the agent's current state.
96.      * Used in index.xhtml to centralise the conditional class logic.
97.      */
98.     public String getAgentCardClass(Agent agent) {
99.         StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder("agent-card");
100.         if (agent.isActive()) {
101.             sb.append(" active");
102.         } else if (agent.isDone()) {
103.             sb.append(" completed");
104.         } else if (agent.isRejected()) {
105.             sb.append(" rejected");
106.         }
107.         return sb.toString();
108.     }
109. 
110.     /**
111.      * Returns the CSS class(es) for an agent's status dot.
112.      */
113.     public String getStatusDotClass(Agent agent) {
114.         if (agent.isActive()) {
115.             return "status-dot active-dot";
116.         } else if (agent.isDone()) {
117.             return "status-dot done-dot";
118.         } else if (agent.isRejected()) {
119.             return "status-dot rejected-dot";
120.         }
121.         return "status-dot";

124.     public String getEventTypeBadgeClass(AgentEvent event) {
125.         return switch (event.getEventType()) {
126.             case "assistant_message" -> "event-type event-type-assistant";
127.             case "tool_call" -> "event-type event-type-tool-call";
128.             case "tool_result" -> "event-type event-type-tool-result";
129.             case "phase_change" -> "event-type event-type-phase";
130.             case "session_error" -> "event-type event-type-error";
131.             default -> "event-type";
132.         };
133.     }

```
1. package com.microsoft.build.realestate;
2. 
3. import jakarta.enterprise.context.ApplicationScoped;
4. import jakarta.faces.push.Push;
5. import jakarta.faces.push.PushContext;
6. import jakarta.inject.Inject;
7. 
8. /**
9.  * CDI bean wrapping the Jakarta Faces PushContext for the pipeline channel.
10.  * Can be called from any thread (including virtual threads running agent sessions)
11.  * because PushContext.send() is thread-safe when the bean is @ApplicationScoped.
12.  *
13.  * <p>Message format sent to the browser: {@code "agentId:eventType"}
14.  * <ul>
15.  *   <li>{@code "agentId:phase-changed"} — agent moved to a new phase</li>
16.  *   <li>{@code "agentId:agent-removed"} — agent was removed from the pipeline</li>
17.  * </ul>
18.  */
19. @ApplicationScoped
20. public class UiUpdateSocket {
21. 
22.     @Inject
23.     @Push(channel = "pipelineChannel")
24.     private PushContext pushContext;
25. 
26.     /**
27.      * Pushes a phase-change notification for the given agent to all connected browsers.
28.      */
29.     public void pushPhaseChange(String agentId) {
30.         pushContext.send(agentId + ":phase-changed");
31.     }
32. 
33.     /**
34.      * Pushes a removal notification for the given agent to all connected browsers.
35.      * Called when a rejected agent is removed from the pipeline after its linger period.
36.      */
37.     public void pushAgentRemoved(String agentId) {
38.         pushContext.send(agentId + ":agent-removed");
39.     }
40. }
41.
```

</details>

<sub>26m 32s</sub>

### `view`

**view the file at C:\Users\edburns\workareas\review-copilot-pr-22\src\java-agent-orchestrator\src\main\webapp\resources\js\pipeline.js.**

C:\Users\edburns\workareas\review-copilot-pr-22\src\java-agent-orchestrator\src\main\webapp\resources\js\pipeline.js

<details>
<summary>98 lines</summary>

```
1. /**
2.  * pipeline.js — Real Estate Agent Pipeline UI (issue 3.6)
3.  *
4.  * Implements the WebSocket → remoteCommand → partial update → CSS transition chain:
5.  *
6.  *   1. f:websocket calls handlePipelinePush(message) when the server pushes
7.  *   2. handlePipelinePush calls refreshPipeline() (p:remoteCommand)
8.  *   3. PrimeFaces re-renders the pipelineGrid via partial update
9.  *   4. oncomplete fires onPipelineRefreshed() which applies CSS animation classes
10.  */
11. 
12. 'use strict';
13. 
14. /**
15.  * Called by the f:websocket onmessage handler when the server sends a push event.
16.  *
17.  * Message format is "agentId:eventType" (e.g. "a3f1b2c4:phase-changed").
18.  * Per the issue 3.6 spec, the full grid is refreshed on any message regardless of
19.  * event type — the server-side render reflects the current state for all agents.
20.  * This avoids complex client-side state management while remaining correct.
21.  *
22.  * @param {string} message - Server push message (agentId:eventType).
23.  *   Known eventTypes: "phase-changed", "agent-removed"
24.  */
25. function handlePipelinePush(message) {
26.     console.log('[Pipeline] WebSocket push received:', message);
27. 
28.     // Trigger server-side re-render via the p:remoteCommand bridge.
29.     // refreshPipeline() is defined by PrimeFaces as a JS function that
30.     // triggers an Ajax request to re-render the pipelineGrid component.
31.     if (typeof refreshPipeline === 'function') {
32.         refreshPipeline();
33.     } else {
34.         console.warn('[Pipeline] refreshPipeline() not yet available, retrying...');
35.         // Retry after a brief delay in case PrimeFaces hasn't initialised yet
36.         setTimeout(function () {
37.             if (typeof refreshPipeline === 'function') {
38.                 refreshPipeline();
39.             } else {
40.                 console.error('[Pipeline] refreshPipeline() still unavailable after retry. ' +
41.                     'Check that p:remoteCommand name="refreshPipeline" is present in the form.');
42.             }
43.         }, 250);
44.     }
45. }
46. 
47. /**
48.  * Called by the p:remoteCommand oncomplete callback AFTER PrimeFaces has
49.  * finished updating the DOM for the pipelineGrid.
50.  *
51.  * This is the correct place to apply CSS animation classes because at this
52.  * point the server-rendered HTML is already in the DOM.
53.  */
54. function onPipelineRefreshed() {
55.     console.log('[Pipeline] DOM updated — applying animation classes.');
56. 
57.     var cards = document.querySelectorAll('.agent-card');
58. 
59.     cards.forEach(function (card) {
60.         var active = card.getAttribute('data-active') === 'true';
61.         var rejected = card.getAttribute('data-rejected') === 'true';
62.         var done = card.getAttribute('data-done') === 'true';
63. 
64.         // Remove existing state classes before reapplying
65.         card.classList.remove('active', 'completed', 'rejected');
66. 
67.         if (rejected) {
68.             card.classList.add('rejected');
69.         } else if (done) {
70.             card.classList.add('completed');
71.         } else if (active) {
72.             card.classList.add('active');
73.         }
74. 
75.         // Apply the transitioning class briefly to produce a visible scale effect.
76.         // Cancel any previously scheduled removal to avoid stale timers overwriting new transitions.
77.         if (card._transitionTimer) {
78.             clearTimeout(card._transitionTimer);
79.         }
80.         card.classList.add('transitioning');
81.         card._transitionTimer = setTimeout(function () {
82.             card.classList.remove('transitioning');
83.             card._transitionTimer = null;
84.         }, 400);
85.     });
86. 
87.     // Update pulse indicators: all currently-active cards' status dots pulse
88.     var allDots = document.querySelectorAll('.status-dot');
89.     allDots.forEach(function (dot) {
90.         dot.classList.remove('pulse-indicator');
91.     });
92. 
93.     var activeDots = document.querySelectorAll('.agent-card.active .status-dot');
94.     activeDots.forEach(function (dot) {
95.         dot.classList.add('pulse-indicator');
96.     });
97. }
98.
```

</details>

=== New Line Comments (from Copilot only) ===
{"body":"`event.timestamp`, `event.eventType`, and especially `event.summary` are rendered via raw Facelets template text (`#{...}`) rather than `\u003ch:outputText\u003e`. If any of these values ever contain `\u003c`, `\u0026`, or quotes (e.g., from future event sources), they will be emitted unescaped and can break markup or enable HTML injection. Use `\u003ch:outputText\u003e` to ensure escaping is consistently applied.","id":3548321219,"line":null,"path":"src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/webapp/index.xhtml"}
{"body":"Trimming the bounded `events` list with `while (events.size() \u003e MAX_EVENTS) { events.remove(0); }` can be unnecessarily expensive on `CopyOnWriteArrayList` because each `remove(0)` forces an array copy/shift. Clearing the excess range in one operation avoids repeated copying and scales better if event volume increases.","id":3548321239,"line":262,"path":"src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/Agent.java"}
{"body":"`AppState` is `@ApplicationScoped`, so storing `selectedAgentId` here makes the “selected agent” a single global value shared across all browser sessions. In a multi-client demo this means one user’s click will change which agent details are rendered for every other connected user (and will be pushed to them via the shared refresh flow). Move selection state to a per-user scope (e.g., `@SessionScoped`/`@ViewScoped` backing bean) and have it look up the `Agent` in `AppState` rather than keeping the selection in application state.","id":3548361722,"line":34,"path":"src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/AppState.java"}
{"body":"This change triggers `notifyUi()` (which pushes a `:phase-changed` message) for every Copilot session event, not just actual phase changes. Because the client refresh cycle animates *all* cards on every `refreshPipeline()` completion, frequent non-phase events (tool calls/results, assistant messages, etc.) can cause constant re-render + animation churn and unnecessary server push traffic. Consider emitting a distinct push event type for “detail updated” (or throttling/batching updates) and only running the phase-change animation path when a real phase transition occurs.","id":3548361743,"line":132,"path":"src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/Agent.java"}

{"body":"`events` uses CopyOnWriteArrayList, but `addEvent()` also synchronizes on the list instance for compound add+trim. CopyOnWriteArrayList is optimized for many readers / few writers, so per-event writes can cause unnecessary array copying. Also, synchronizing on the list object doesn’t align with CopyOnWriteArrayList’s internal lock, so the synchronized block can be misleading if it’s intended to provide atomicity. Consider switching to a write-optimized bounded structure (e.g., ArrayDeque guarded by a private lock, or another bounded queue) and copying to an immutable List in `getEvents()`.","id":3548402974,"line":48,"path":"src/java-agent-orchestrator/src/main/java/com/microsoft/build/realestate/Agent.java"}

C:\Users\edburns\workareas\review-copilot-pr-22\src\java-agent-orchestrator\src\main\java\com\microsoft\build\realestate\UiUpdateSocket.java

<details>
<summary>50 lines</summary>

```
1. package com.microsoft.build.realestate;
2. 
3. import jakarta.enterprise.context.ApplicationScoped;
4. import jakarta.faces.push.Push;
5. import jakarta.faces.push.PushContext;
6. import jakarta.inject.Inject;
7. 
8. /**
9.  * CDI bean wrapping the Jakarta Faces PushContext for the pipeline channel.
10.  * Can be called from any thread (including virtual threads running agent sessions)
11.  * because PushContext.send() is thread-safe when the bean is @ApplicationScoped.
12.  *
13.  * <p>Message format sent to the browser: {@code "agentId:eventType"}
14.  * <ul>
15.  *   <li>{@code "agentId:phase-changed"} — agent moved to a new phase</li>
16.  *   <li>{@code "agentId:agent-removed"} — agent was removed from the pipeline</li>
17.  * </ul>
18.  */
19. @ApplicationScoped
20. public class UiUpdateSocket {
21. 
22.     @Inject
23.     @Push(channel = "pipelineChannel")
24.     private PushContext pushContext;
25. 
26.     /**
27.      * Pushes a phase-change notification for the given agent to all connected browsers.
28.      */
29.     public void pushPhaseChange(String agentId) {
30.         pushContext.send(agentId + ":phase-changed");
31.     }
32. 
33.     /**
34.      * Pushes a detail-update notification for the given agent to all connected browsers.
35.      * Called when new session events are captured (tool calls, assistant messages, etc.)
36.      * so only the detail panel refreshes without triggering full-grid card animations.
37.      */
38.     public void pushDetailUpdate(String agentId) {
39.         pushContext.send(agentId + ":detail-updated");
40.     }
41. 
42.     /**
43.      * Pushes a removal notification for the given agent to all connected browsers.
44.      * Called when a rejected agent is removed from the pipeline after its linger period.
45.      */
46.     public void pushAgentRemoved(String agentId) {
47.         pushContext.send(agentId + ":agent-removed");
48.     }
49. }
50.
```

</details>

181.     private void captureSessionEvent(Object event) {
182.         if (event == null) {
183.             return;
184.         }
185.         String eventClassName = event.getClass().getSimpleName();
186.         switch (eventClassName) {
187.             case "AssistantMessageEvent" -> captureAssistantMessageEvent(event);
188.             case "ToolExecutionStartEvent" -> captureToolExecutionStart(event);
189.             case "ToolExecutionCompleteEvent" -> captureToolExecutionComplete(event);
190.             default -> addEvent(Instant.now(), "session_event", eventClassName, event.toString());
191.         }
192.     }

2.  * pipeline.js — Real Estate Agent Pipeline UI (issue 3.6)

6.  *

9.  *     2. handlePipelinePush calls refreshPipeline() (p:remoteCommand)

287. 
288.     private static Collection<?> asIterable(Object value) {
289.         if (value instanceof Collection<?> collection) {
290.             return collection;
291.         }
292.         if (value instanceof Object[] array) {
293.             return List.of(array);
294.         }
295.         return List.of();
296.     }
297. 
298.     private static String nullSafe(String value, String fallback) {
299.         return value == null || value.isBlank() ? fallback : value;
